Our thriving and exciting city is not just home to Amy, but also to places like the Country Music Hall of Fame, the incomparable Schermerhorn Symphony Center, and the world-famous Ryman Auditorium, to world-class shopping and dining that have put Nashville on the map as the new \"it\" city according to the New York Times, and certainly to some of the world's best music! Come be our guests as Amy brings us all together for a weekend of music and memories in the heart of downtown Nashville! But, of course, we'll sneak away from the big city for some fun on the farm as well, so don't forget to bring your boots! We can't wait to see you next year! In the meantime, here are some of the basics.\nAMY GRANT'S NASHVILLE WEEKEND 2015\n* Weekend Proceeds To Benefit THE HELPING HANDS FOUNDATION\n* Date: Friday, September 18 to Sunday, September 20, 2015\n* FOA/Previous Weekend Attendee Pre-sale: Wednesday, December 3, 2014 @ 10 am central central on iTickets.com\n* General Public On-sale: Friday, December 1, 2014 @ 10 am central\n* Event Website Launch with Full FAQ: Tuesday,December 2, 2014 @ 1 pm central on AmyGrant.com\n* Price: $449.00 plus ticket ($29.95) and sales tax (payment plans will be available to assist guests in making their reservations - at time of booking you will be able to make a deposit of 15% plus ticket fee and sales tax - to reserve your spot).\n* Schedule:\n* Friday Night Welcome Reception & Concert: AT THE COUNTRY MUSIC HALL OF FAME'S CMA THEATRE (featuring a special Storyteller Concert by AMY GRANT, never before staged)\n* Friday Late Night: Suggested Late Night group activity will be available for Night-Owls\n* Saturday morning @ ROCKETOWN (featuring a special guest speaker and speaking/music by AMY GRANT; and a morning breakfast snack reception and tours of Rocketown)\n* Saturday afternoon: Free time in Downtown Nashville and shuttles to farm\n* Saturday Afternoon/Evening: AMY'S FARM (featuring a concert by AMY GRANT & FRIENDS; Campfire Songs; and some of our favorite events from the past and other new activities)\n* Sunday Morning: SCHERMERHORN SYMPHONY CENTER (featuring a message and music from Amy and a morning breakfast snack reception)\n* Official Hotel: We will have suggested hotels available for guests to reserve whatever type of room you want and fits your budget for the weekend\n* BASIC Logistics and Travel: We will provide shuttles to/from Downtown Nashville to Rocketown and to Amy's Farm during the weekend (exact pick-up and drop-off will be announced as we get closer to the event weekend) - Pick-up/Drop-off location will be within walking distance of most Downtown Nashville hotels near Broadway and 4th Avenue (near the Country Music Hall of Fame). We suggest that you have your flights arrive into Nashville on Friday, September 18th before 5 pm.
